87.05 Special purpose motor vehicles, other than 
those principally designed for the 
transport of persons or goods (for 
example, breakdown lorries, crane lorries, 
fire fighting vehicles, concrete-mixer 
lorries, road sweeper lorries, spraying 
lorries, mobile workshops, mobile
